-- Creating schema and table for ticket_sales_physical
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE ticket_sales_physical (
  payment_method STRING,
  purchase_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  discount_percent INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  purchase_channel STRING,
  ticket_price INT,
  purchase_date DATE,
  ticket_id INT,
  visit_date DATE,
  customer_id INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  visit_hour INT,
  is_online_sale BOOLEAN,
  sale_id INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for ticket_sales_online
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE ticket_sales_online (
  payment_method STRING,
  purchase_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  discount_percent INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  purchase_channel STRING,
  ticket_price INT,
  purchase_date DATE,
  ticket_id INT,
  visit_date DATE,
  customer_id INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  visit_hour INT,
  is_online_sale BOOLEAN,
  sale_id INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for merchandise_sales_physical
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE merchandise_sales_physical (
  payment_method STRING,
  sale_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  quantity INT,
  product_name STRING,
  total_price INT,
  sale_date DATE,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  unit_price INT,
  staff_member STRING,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  category STRING,
  customer_id INT,
  discount_applied INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  product_id INT,
  sale_id INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for merchandise_sales_online
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE merchandise_sales_online (
  payment_method STRING,
  sale_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  quantity INT,
  product_name STRING,
  total_price INT,
  sale_date DATE,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  unit_price INT,
  staff_member FLOAT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  category STRING,
  customer_id INT,
  discount_applied INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  product_id INT,
  sale_id INT
);

  house_status STRING,
  duration_minutes INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for maintenance_costs
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS park_internal;
USE SCHEMA park_internal;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE maintenance_costs (
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  date TIMESTAMP,
  maintenance_cost INT,
  equipment_maintenance INT,
  prop_repairs INT,
  structural_repairs INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  maintenance_type STRING,
  cost_id INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for supplies_costs
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS park_internal;
USE SCHEMA park_internal;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE supplies_costs (
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  prop_supplies INT,
  supplier STRING,
  makeup_supplies INT,
  date TIMESTAMP,
  costume_supplies INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  cleaning_supplies INT,
  supplies_cost INT,
  cost_id INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for staff_costs
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS park_internal;
USE SCHEMA park_internal;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE staff_costs (
  security_staff INT,
  supervisor_salary INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  maintenance_staff INT,
  overtime_hours INT,
  date TIMESTAMP,
  staff_cost INT,
  staff_count INT,
  actor_salaries INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  cost_id INT
);

  theme STRING,

  house_size_sqft INT,

  house_name STRING,
  duration_minutes INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  max_capacity_per_group INT,
  fear_level INT,
  haunted_house_id INT
);
